NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE
MARUTTI BUILD TECH
“That on 27-01-2017 S. Lata wife of Selvamani, residing at No.82, VOC Street, Vengamedu, Karur has retired from
M/s. Marutti Build Tech having office at No.157E, M.G. Road, Bharathi Nagar, Karur-2 and on 27-01-2017 M/s. Marutti Build
Tech firm has now reconstituted with it’s existing partners namely 1. N. Baskar, 2. S. Karthik, 3. K. Kanimozhi
and 4. K. Tamilselvi.”
Karur,

For Marutti Build Tech,

10th February 2017.

S. KARTHIK,
Managing Partner.

I. KARTHIK a Male Child born on Thiru R. IRULAPPAN, on 10-05-1992 residing at No.2, New Street, M.M. Colony,
Aminjikarai, Chennai-600 029, has been living as transgender after an elaborate Sexual reassignment Surgery by
Dr. V. Jeyaraman, S.Mch. MNAMs., Dip.N.B.,Ph.D.,FICS, Professor of Plastic Surgery, KMC, Ch-10. By this I, may be treated
as a transgender and shall henceforth be known as S. DEEPIKA.

Chennai,

I. KARTHIK.

10th February 2017.
